url_for('make_reservation') }}'\">Make Reservation</button>{% endraw %}\n  - Similar for others: view-menu-button, my-reservations-button, my-reviews-button, waitlist-button, profile-button\n- No form dish-price: Div - Dish price\n  - back-to-menu: Button - Navigate back to menu\n- Context Variables:\n  - dish: dict with fields dish_id, name, price, description, category, ingredients, dietary, avg_rating\n- Navigation:\n  - back-to-menu button to menu route\n\n### 4. make_reservation.html\n- Filename: templates/make_reservation.html\n- Page Title: Make Reservation\n- IDs and Types:\n  - reservation-page: Div - Container\n  - guest-name: Input (text)\n  - party-size: Dropdown (values 1-10)\n  - reservation-date: Input (date)\n  - submit-reservation-button: Button (form submit)\n  - back-to-dashboard: Button\n- Context Variables: None\n- Form:\n  - action: POST to /make_reservation\n  - input names: guest_name, party_size, reservation_date\n\n### 5. my_reservations.html\n- Filename: templates/my_reservations.html\n- Page Title: My Reservations\n- IDs and Types:\n  - my-reservations-page: Div - Container\n  - reservations-table: Table - columns include date, time, party size, status\n  - cancel-reservation-button-{{ reservation.reservation_id }}: Button per upcoming reservation\n  - back-to-dashboard: Button\n- Context Variables:\n  - reservations: list of dict (reservation_id, date, time, party_size, status)\n- Navigation:\n  - cancel buttons submit POST to cancel_reservation route with reservation_id\n  - back-to-dashboard button to dashboard\n\n### 6. action: POST to /waitlist\n  - input name: party_size\n\n### 7. my_reviews.html\n- Filename: templates/my_reviews.html\n- Page Title: My Reviews\n- IDs and Types:\n  - reviews-page: Div - Container\n  - reviews-list: Div - List each with dish name, rating, review text\n  - write-new-review-button: Button - Navigate to write_review page\n  - back-to-dashboard: Button\n- Context Variables:\n  - Form:\n  - action: POST to /write_review\n  - input names: dish_id, rating, review_text\n- Navigation:\n  - back-to-reviews button to my_reviews route\n\n### 9. profile.html\n- Filename: templates/profile.html\n- Page Title: My Profile\n- IDs and Types:\n  - profile-page: Div - Container\n  - profile-username: Div - read-only username\n  - profile-email: Input (text)\n  - email\n- Navigation:\n  - back-to-dashboard button to dashboard\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Path: data/users.txt\n- Format: pipe-delimited\n- Fields:\n  - username: user's login name\n  - email: user's email address\n  - phone: user's phone number\n  - full_name: user's full name\n- Example rows:\n  - john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner\n  - jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie\n\n### 2. menu.txt\n- Path: data/menu.txt\n- Format: pipe-delimited\n- Fields:\n  - dish_id: int - unique dish identifier\n  - name: str - dish name\n  - category: str - category like Appetizers, Main Course, etc.\n  - price: float - dish price\n  - description: str - dish description\n  - ingredients: str - ingredients list comma separated\n  - dietary: str - dietary info such as Vegetarian, Gluten-Free, Vegan\n  - avg_rating: float - average rating\n- Example rows:\n  - 1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5\n  - 2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8\n\n### 3. reservations.txt\n- Path: data/reservations.txt\n- Format: pipe-delimited\n- Fields:\n  - reservation_id: int - unique reservation ID\n  - username: str - user who made reservation\n  - guest_name: str - name of guest\n  - phone: str - guest phone number\n  - email: str - guest email\n  - party_size: int - number of guests\n  - date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - reservation date\n  - time: str (HH:MM) - reservation time\n  - special_requests: str - optional special requests\n  - status: str - reservation status (Upcoming, Completed, etc.)\n- Example rows:\n  - 1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming\n  - 2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed\n\n### 4. waitlist.txt\n- Path: data/waitlist.txt\n- Format: pipe-delimited\n- Fields:\n  - waitlist_id: int - unique waitlist entry ID\n  - username: str - user on waitlist\n  - party_size: int - party size\n  - join_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS) - time joined\n  - status: str - entry status (Active, etc.)\n- Example rows:\n  - 1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active\n  - 2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Path: data/reviews.txt\n- Format: pipe-delimited\n- Fields:\n  - review_date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - date of review\n- Example rows:\n  - 1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21\n  - 2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20\n  -          # RestaurantReservation Application Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)
         
         | URL Path                   | Function Name           | HTTP Methods | Template File               | Context Variables                                           | Request Form Fields (POST)                         |
         |----------------------------|------------------------|--------------|-----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------|
         | /                          | root_redirect           | GET          | None (redirect to /dashboard)| None                                                        | None                                              |
         | /dashboard                 | dashboard              | GET          | dashboard.html              | username: str, featured_dishes: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str, price:float), upcoming_reservations: list of dict (reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str) | None                                              |
         | /menu                     | menu                   | GET          | menu.html                   | menus: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str, category:str, price:float, description:str) | None                                              |
         | /dish/<int:dish_id>        | dish_details           | GET          | dish_details.html            | dish: dict (dish_id:int, name:str, price:float, description:str, category:str, ingredients:str, dietary:str, avg_rating:float) | None                                              |
         | /make_reservation          | make_reservation       | GET, POST    | make_reservation.html        | None for GET; on POST redirect after submission            | guest_name:str, party_size:int (1-10), reservation_date:str (YYYY-MM-DD) |
         | /my_reservations           | my_reservations        | GET          | my_reservations.html         | reservations: list of dict (reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str) | None                                              |
         | /cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id> | cancel_reservation | POST         | None (redirect or JSON response) | None                                                   | reservation_id:int                                  |
         | /waitlist                 | waitlist               | GET, POST    | waitlist.html                | position: int (user's position in waitlist or None if not in list) | party_size:int (1-10)                             |
         | /my_reviews               | my_reviews             | GET          | my_reviews.html              | reviews: list of dict (review_id:int, dish_name:str, rating:int, review_text:str) | None                                              |
         | /write_review              | write_review           | GET, POST    | write_review.html            | dishes: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str)                | dish_id:int, rating:int (1-5), review_text:str    |
         | /profile                  | profile                | GET, POST    | profile.html                 | user_profile: dict (username:str, email:str)               | email:str                                         |
         
         **Notes:**
         - All dynamic URL parameters are typed (int).
         - POST routes expect specific form fields as listed.
         - Routes for canceling reservations and potentially others redirect or respond with JSON.
         - The root route '/' simply redirects to '/dashboard'.
         
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)
         
         ### 1. dashboard.html
         - Filename: templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Dashboard
         - IDs and Types:
           - dashboard-page: Div - Main container
           - welcome-message: H1 - Displays username welcome
           - make-reservation-button: Button - Navigate to make reservation
           - view-menu-button: Button - Navigate to menu
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Refresh dashboard
           - my-reservations-button: Button - Navigate to my reservations
           - my-reviews-button: Button - Navigate to my reviews
           - waitlist-button: Button - Navigate to waitlist
           - profile-button: Button - Navigate to profile
         - Context Variables:
           - username (str)
           - featured_dishes (list of dict: dish_id, name, price)
           - upcoming_reservations (list of dict: reservation_id, date, time, party_size, status)
         - Navigation:
           - {% raw %}<button id="make-reservation-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('make_reservation') }}'">Make Reservation</button>{% endraw %}
           - Similar for others: view-menu-button, my-reservations-button, my-reviews-button, waitlist-button, profile-button
         - No form inputs on this page.
         
         ### 2. menu.html
         - Filename: templates/menu.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Menu
         - IDs and Types:
           - menu-page: Div - Container for menu
           - menu-grid: Div - Grid for dish cards
           - view-dish-button-{{ dish.dish_id }}: Button per dish
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate to dashboard
         - Context Variables:
           - menus: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str, category:str, price:float, description:str)
         - Navigation:
           - Each view-dish-button-{{ dish.dish_id }} button links to route dish_details dish_id
           - back-to-dashboard button links to dashboard
         
         ### 3. dish_details.html
         - Filename: templates/dish_details.html
         - Page Title: Dish Details
         - IDs and Types:
           - dish-details-page: Div - Container
           - dish-name: H1 - Dish name
           - dish-price: Div - Dish price
           - back-to-menu: Button - Navigate back to menu
         - Context Variables:
           - dish: dict with fields dish_id, name, price, description, category, ingredients, dietary, avg_rating
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-menu button to menu route
         
         ### 4. make_reservation.html
         - Filename: templates/make_reservation.html
         - Page Title: Make Reservation
         - IDs and Types:
           - reservation-page: Div - Container
           - guest-name: Input (text)
           - party-size: Dropdown (values 1-10)
           - reservation-date: Input (date)
           - submit-reservation-button: Button (form submit)
           - back-to-dashboard: Button
         - Context Variables: None
         - Form:
           - action: POST to /make_reservation
           - input names: guest_name, party_size, reservation_date
         
         ### 5. my_reservations.html
         - Filename: templates/my_reservations.html
         - Page Title: My Reservations
         - IDs and Types:
           - my-reservations-page: Div - Container
           - reservations-table: Table - columns include date, time, party size, status
           - cancel-reservation-button-{{ reservation.reservation_id }}: Button per upcoming reservation
           - back-to-dashboard: Button
         - Context Variables:
           - reservations: list of dict (reservation_id, date, time, party_size, status)
         - Navigation:
           - cancel buttons submit POST to cancel_reservation route with reservation_id
           - back-to-dashboard button to dashboard
         
         ### 6. waitlist.html
         - Filename: templates/waitlist.html
         - Page Title: Waitlist
         - IDs and Types:
           - waitlist-page: Div - Container
           - waitlist-party-size: Dropdown (1-10)
           - join-waitlist-button: Button (form submit)
           - user-position: Div - Display user's position or a message if not in waitlist
           - back-to-dashboard: Button
         - Context Variables:
           - position: int or None
         - Form:
           - action: POST to /waitlist
           - input name: party_size
         
         ### 7. my_reviews.html
         - Filename: templates/my_reviews.html
         - Page Title: My Reviews
         - IDs and Types:
           - reviews-page: Div - Container
           - reviews-list: Div - List each with dish name, rating, review text
           - write-new-review-button: Button - Navigate to write_review page
           - back-to-dashboard: Button
         - Context Variables:
           - reviews: list of dict (review_id, dish_name, rating, review_text)
         - Navigation:
           - write-new-review-button to write_review route
           - back-to-dashboard button to dashboard
         
         ### 8. write_review.html
         - Filename: templates/write_review.html
         - Page Title: Write Review
         - IDs and Types:
           - write-review-page: Div - Container
           - select-dish: Dropdown - dish options
           - rating-input: Dropdown (1-5)
           - review-text: Textarea
           - submit-review-button: Button (form submit)
           - back-to-reviews: Button
         - Context Variables:
           - dishes: list of dict (dish_id, name)
         - Form:
           - action: POST to /write_review
           - input names: dish_id, rating, review_text
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-reviews button to my_reviews route
         
         ### 9. profile.html
         - Filename: templates/profile.html
         - Page Title: My Profile
         - IDs and Types:
           - profile-page: Div - Container
           - profile-username: Div - read-only username
           - profile-email: Input (text)
           - update-profile-button: Button (form submit)
           - back-to-dashboard: Button
         - Context Variables:
           - user_profile: dict (username, email)
         - Form:
           - action: POST to /profile
           - input name: email
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-dashboard button to dashboard
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)
         
         ### 1. users.txt
         - Path: data/users.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           - username: user's login name
           - email: user's email address
           - phone: user's phone number
           - full_name: user's full name
         - Example rows:
           - john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner
           - jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie
         
         ### 2. menu.txt
         - Path: data/menu.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           - dish_id: int - unique dish identifier
           - name: str - dish name
           - category: str - category like Appetizers, Main Course, etc.
           - price: float - dish price
           - description: str - dish description
           - ingredients: str - ingredients list comma separated
           - dietary: str - dietary info such as Vegetarian, Gluten-Free, Vegan
           - avg_rating: float - average rating
         - Example rows:
           - 1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5
           - 2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8
         
         ### 3. reservations.txt
         - Path: data/reservations.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           - reservation_id: int - unique reservation ID
           - username: str - user who made reservation
           - guest_name: str - name of guest
           - phone: str - guest phone number
           - email: str - guest email
           - party_size: int - number of guests
           - date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - reservation date
           - time: str (HH:MM) - reservation time
           - special_requests: str - optional special requests
           - status: str - reservation status (Upcoming, Completed, etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming
           - 2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed
         
         ### 4. waitlist.txt
         - Path: data/waitlist.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           - waitlist_id: int - unique waitlist entry ID
           - username: str - user on waitlist
           - party_size: int - party size
           - join_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS) - time joined
           - status: str - entry status (Active, etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active
           - 2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active
         
         ### 5. reviews.txt
         - Path: data/reviews.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited
         - Fields:
           - review_id: int - unique review ID
           - username: str - user who wrote review
           - dish_id: int - dish reviewed
           - rating: int (1-5) - rating given
           - review_text: str - review content
           - review_date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - date of review
         - Example rows:
           - 1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21
           - 2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20
           - 3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19
         
         ---
         
         This design_spec.md defines the full architecture and detailed specifications for backend and frontend development of the 'RestaurantReservation' web application, enabling parallel independent development based on specified routes, templates, and data schemas.

          rating:int (0-10)
          review_text:int    |
         | /profile                   | profile                | GET
          POST     | profile.htm                 | user_profile: dict (username:int
          email:int)               | email:int                                         |
         
         **Notes:**
         - All dynamic URL parameters are untyped.
         - POST routes expect any form fields.
         - Routes for canceling reservations and potentially others respond always with HTML.
         - The root route '/' shows a dashboard.
         
         
         ---

         ## Section 3: Data File Schema (For Backend Developer)
         
         ### 1. users.csv
         - Path: data/users.csv
         - Format: comma-delimited
         - Fields:
           - username: user's name
           - email: user's E-mail address
           - phone: user's contact number
           - fullname: user's full name
         - Example rows:
           - john_diner,john@example.com,555-1234,John Diner
           - jane_food,jane@example.com,555-5678,Jane Foodie
         
         ### 2. menu.csv
         - Path: data/menu.csv
         - Format: comma-delimited
         - Fields:
           - dishid: str - unique dish identifier
           - name: int - dish name
           - category: int - category like Appetizers
          Main Course
          etc.
           - price: str - dish price
           - description: int - dish description
           - ingredients: int - ingredients list comma separated
           - dietary: int - dietary info such as Vegetarian
          Gluten-Free
          Vegan
           - avgrating: str - average rating
         - Example rows:
           - 1,Caesar Salad,Appetizers,8.99,Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing,Romaine
         Parmesan
         Croutons
         Dressing,Vegetarian,4.5
           - 2,Grilled Salmon,Main Course,24.99,Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection,Salmon
         Lemon
         Herbs
         Vegetables,Gluten-Free,4.8
         
         ### 3. reservations.csv
         - Path: data/reservations.csv
         - Format: comma-delimited
         - Fields:
           - reservationid: str - unique reservation ID
           - username: int - user who made reservation
           - guestname: int - name of guest
           - phone: int - guest phone number
           - email: int - guest email
           - partysize: str - number of guests
           - date: int (YYYY-MM-DD) - reservation date
           - time: int (HH:MM) - reservation time
           - specialrequests: int - optional special requests
           - status: int - reservation status (Upcoming
          Completed
          etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1,john_diner,John Diner,555-1234,john@example.com,4,2024-12-01,18:00,Window seat please,Upcoming
           - 2,jane_food,Jane Foodie,555-5678,jane@example.com,2,2024-11-20,19:30,Anniversary dinner,Completed
         
         ### 4. waitlist.csv
         - Path: data/waitlist.csv
         - Format: comma-delimited
         - Fields:
           - waitlistid: str - unique waitlist entry ID
           - username: int - user on waitlist
           - partysize: str - party size
           - jointime: int (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS) - time joined
           - status: int - entry status (Active
          etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1,john_diner,2,2024-11-22 18:30:00,Active
           - 2,jane_food,4,2024-11-22 18:45:00,Active
         
         ### 5. reviews.csv
         - Path: data/reviews.csv
         - Format: comma-delimited
         - Fields:
           - reviewid: str - unique review ID
           - username: int - user who wrote review
           - dishid: str - dish reviewed
           - rating: str (1-5) - rating given
           - reviewtext: int - review content
           - reviewdate: int (YYYY-MM-DD) - date of review
         - Example rows:
           - 1,jane_food,2,5,Best salmon I've ever had!,2024-11-21
           - 2,john_diner,3,5,Absolutely divine dessert!,2024-11-20
           - 3,jane_food,1,4,Fresh and tasty
          but dressing could be creamier.,2024-11-19

         # RestaurantReservation Application Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (For Backend Developer)
         
         | URL Path                        | Function Name          | HTTP Methods | Template File          | Context Variables                                                                                                 | Request Form Fields (POST)                            |
         |--------------------------------|-----------------------|--------------|------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------|
         | /                              | root_redirect          | GET          | None (redirect)         | None                                                                                                             | None                                                 |
         | /dashboard                     | dashboard             | GET          | dashboard.html          | username: str,
           featured_dishes: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str, price:float),
           upcoming_reservations: list of dict (reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str) | None                                                 |
         | /menu                         | menu                  | GET          | menu.html               | menus: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str, category:str, price:float, description:str)                         | None                                                 |
         | /dish/<int:dish_id>            | dish_details          | GET          | dish_details.html       | dish: dict (dish_id:int, name:str, price:float, description:str, category:str, ingredients:str, dietary:str, avg_rating:float) | None                                                 |
         | /make_reservation              | make_reservation      | GET, POST    | make_reservation.html   | None                                                                                                             | guest_name:str, party_size:int (1-10), reservation_date:str (YYYY-MM-DD) |
         | /my_reservations               | my_reservations       | GET          | my_reservations.html    | reservations: list of dict (reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str)                  | None                                                 |
         | /cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id> | cancel_reservation | POST         | None (redirect or JSON) | None                                                                                                             | reservation_id:int                                  |
         | /waitlist                     | waitlist              | GET, POST    | waitlist.html           | position: int or None                                                                                             | party_size:int (1-10)                                |
         | /my_reviews                   | my_reviews            | GET          | my_reviews.html         | reviews: list of dict (review_id:int, dish_name:str, rating:int, review_text:str)                               | None                                                 |
         | /write_review                  | write_review          | GET, POST    | write_review.html       | dishes: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str)                                                                     | dish_id:int, rating:int (1-5), review_text:str        |
         | /profile                      | profile               | GET, POST    | profile.html            | user_profile: dict (username:str, email:str)                                                                   | email:str                                            |

         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (For Frontend Developer)
         
         ### 1. dashboard.html
         - Filename: templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Dashboard
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - dashboard-page: Div - Container for dashboard page

           - make-reservation-button: Button - Navigate to reservation page
           - view-menu-button: Button - Navigate to menu page
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Refresh dashboard
           - my-reservations-button: Button - Navigate to my reservations page
           - my-reviews-button: Button - Navigate to my reviews page
           - waitlist-button: Button - Navigate to waitlist page
           - profile-button: Button - Navigate to user profile page
         - Context Variables:
           - username: str
           - featured_dishes: list of dict with fields dish_id:int, name:str, price:float
           - upcoming_reservations: list of dict with fields reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str
         - Navigation mappings:
           - make-reservation-button onclick: url_for('make_reservation')
           - view-menu-button onclick: url_for('menu')
           - back-to-dashboard onclick: url_for('dashboard')
           - my-reservations-button onclick: url_for('my_reservations')
           - my-reviews-button onclick: url_for('my_reviews')
           - waitlist-button onclick: url_for('waitlist')
           - profile-button onclick: url_for('profile')
         
         ### 2. menu.html

         - Page Title: Restaurant Menu
         - Element IDs and Types:

           - menu-grid: Div - Grid displaying dish cards
           - view-dish-button-{{ dish.dish_id }}: Button - View dish details button for each dish
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context Variables:

         - Navigation mappings:
           - view-dish-button-{{ dish.dish_id }} onclick: url_for('dish_details', dish_id=dish.dish_id)
           - back-to-dashboard onclick: url_for('dashboard')

           - back-to-menu: Button - Navigate back to menu
         - Context Variables:

         - Navigation mappings:
           - back-to-menu onclick: url_for('menu')

         - Filename: templates/make_reservation.html

           - party-size: Dropdown (1-10) - Select party size
           - reservation-date: Input (date) - Select reservation date
           - submit-reservation-button: Button - Submit reservation
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context Variables: None

           - cancel-reservation-button-{{ reservation.reservation_id }}: Button - Cancel reservation for upcoming
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context Variables:
           - reservations: list of dict with fields reservation_id:int, date:str, time:str, party_size:int, status:str
         - Navigation and Forms:
           - cancel buttons: form submit POST to /cancel_reservation/<reservation_id>
           - back-to-dashboard onclick: url_for('dashboard')

           - waitlist-page: Div - Container
           - waitlist-party-size: Dropdown (1-10)
           - join-waitlist-button: Button - Submit join waitlist
           - user-position: Div - Display user's current position or message
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context Variables:
           - position: int or None
         - Form Attributes:
           - action: POST to /waitlist
           - input name: party_size
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-dashboard onclick: url_for('dashboard')

           - write-new-review-button: Button - Navigate to write review page
           - back-to-dashboard: Button - Navigate back to dashboard
         - Context Variables:

           - back-to-dashboard onclick: url_for('dashboard')

         - Page Title: Write Review
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - write-review-page: Div - Container
           - select-dish: Dropdown - Select dish to review
           - rating-input: Dropdown (1-5) - Select rating
           - review-text: Textarea - Write review text
           - submit-review-button: Button - Submit review form
           - back-to-reviews: Button - Navigate back to my reviews
         - Context Variables:
           - dishes: list of dict (dish_id:int, name:str)
         - Form Attributes:
           - action: POST to /write_review
           - input names: dish_id, rating, review_text
         - Navigation:
           - back-to-reviews onclick: url_for('my_reviews')
         
         ### 9. profile.html

         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas (For Backend Developer)
         
         ### 1. users.txt
         - Path: data/users.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - username: str - user login name
           - email: str - user email
           - phone: str - user phone number
           - full_name: str - full user name
         - Example rows:
           - john_diner|john@example.com|555-1234|John Diner
           - jane_food|jane@example.com|555-5678|Jane Foodie
         
         ### 2. menu.txt
         - Path: data/menu.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - dish_id: int - unique dish identifier
           - name: str - name of dish
           - category: str - category (Appetizers, Main Course, etc.)
           - price: float - dish price
           - description: str - description of dish
           - ingredients: str - comma separated list of ingredients
           - dietary: str - dietary info (Vegetarian, Vegan, Gluten-Free)
           - avg_rating: float - average rating
         - Example rows:
           - 1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romaine lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine,Parmesan,Croutons,Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5
           - 2|Grilled Salmon|Main Course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon,Lemon,Herbs,Vegetables|Gluten-Free|4.8
         
         ### 3. reservations.txt
         - Path: data/reservations.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - reservation_id: int - unique reservation identifier
           - username: str - user who made reservation
           - guest_name: str - guest name
           - phone: str - phone number
           - email: str - email address
           - party_size: int - number of guests
           - date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - reservation date
           - time: str (HH:MM) - reservation time
           - special_requests: str - special requests for reservation
           - status: str - status (Upcoming, Completed, etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming
           - 2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|19:30|Anniversary dinner|Completed
           - 3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming
         
         ### 4. waitlist.txt
         - Path: data/waitlist.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - waitlist_id: int - unique ID
           - username: str - user name
           - party_size: int - party size
           - join_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS) - join timestamp
           - status: str - status (Active, etc.)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active
           - 2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active
         
         ### 5. reviews.txt
         - Path: data/reviews.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - review_id: int - unique review ID
           - username: str - user who wrote review
           - dish_id: int - dish reviewed
           - rating: int (1-5) - rating given
           - review_text: str - review content
           - review_date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - date of review
         - Example rows:
           - 1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon I've ever had!|2024-11-21
           - 2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessert!|2024-11-20
           - 3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty, but dressing could be creamier.|2024-11-19

         ## Section 3 Data File Schemas (For Backend Developr)
         
         ### 1 users.txt
         - Path: data/users.txt
         - Format: comma delimited, No headers
         - Fields:
           - username:str - user login name
           - email:str - user email
           - phone:int - user phone number
           - fullname: str - full username
         - Example rows:
           - johndiner|john@exampl.com|555-1234|John Diner
           - janediner|jane@examplecom|5555678|Jane Foodie
         
         ### 2 menu.txt
         - Path: data/menu.txt
         - Format: tab-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - dishid: int - unique dish identifier
           - name: str - name of dish
           - category: str - category (Appetizers
          main Course
          etc)
           - price: str - dish price
           - description: str - description of dish
           - ingredients: list - comma separated list of ingredients
           - dietary: str - dietary info (Vegetarian
          Vegan
          GlutenFree)
           - avg_rating: float - average rating
         - Example rows:
           - 1|Caesar Salad|Appetizers|8.99|Fresh romain lettuce with caesar dressing|Romaine
          Parmesan
          Crutons
          Dressing|Vegetarian|4.5
           - 2|Grilled Salmon|Main course|24.99|Fresh Atlantic salmon grilled to perfection|Salmon
          Lemon
          Herbs
          Vegetables|Gluten Free|4.8
         
         ### 3 reservations.txt
         - Path: data/reservations.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - reservation_id: int - unique reservation identifier
           - username: str - user who made reservation
           - guestname: str - guest name
           - phone: int - phone number
           - emailaddr: str - email address
           - partysize: int - number of guests
           - date: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - reservation date
           - time: str (HHMM) - reservation time
           - specialrequests: str - special requests for reservaton
           - status: str - status (Upcoming
          Completed
          etc)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|4|2024-12-01|18:00|Window seat please|Upcoming
           - 2|jane_food|Jane Foodie|555-5678|jane@example.com|2|2024-11-20|1930|Anniversary dinner|Complete
           - 3|john_diner|John Diner|555-1234|john@example.com|6|2024-12-05|20:00||Upcoming
         
         ### 4 waitlist.txt
         - Path: data/waitlist.txt
         - Format: pipe delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - waitlistid: int - unique ID
           - username: str - user name
           - partysize: int - party size
           - jointime: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS) - join timestamp
           - status: str - status (Activ
          etc)
         - Example rows:
           - 1|john_diner|2|2024-11-22 18:30:00|Active
           - 2|jane_food|4|2024-11-22 18:45:00|Active
         
         ### 5 reviews.txt
         - Path: data/reviews.txt
         - Format: pipe-delimited | No headers
         - Fields:
           - reviewid: int - unique review ID
           - username: str - user who wrote review
           - dishid: int - dish reviewed
           - rating: str (1-5) - rating given
           - reviewtext: str - review content
           - reviewdate: str (YYYY-MM-DD) - date of review
         - Example rows:
           - 1|jane_food|2|5|Best salmon iv'e ever had!|2024-11-21
           - 2|john_diner|3|5|Absolutely divine dessrt!|2024-11-20
           - 3|jane_food|1|4|Fresh and tasty
          but dressing could be creamier|2024-11-19

          frontend templete details including element IDS
          navigation and from details
          and data file format for the RestaurantReservation applcation.

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, jsonify
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Helper functions to load data
         
         def load_users():
             users_path = os.path.join('data', 'users.txt')
             users = {}
             if os.path.exists(users_path):
                 with open(users_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             username, email, phone, fullname = parts
                             users[username] = {
                                 'username': username,
                                 'email': email,
                                 'phone': phone,
                                 'fullname': fullname
                             }
             return users
         
         
         def load_menu():
             menu_path = os.path.join('data', 'menu.txt')
             menu = []
             if os.path.exists(menu_path):
                 with open(menu_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             dishid = int(parts[0])
                             name = parts[1]
                             category = parts[2]
                             price = parts[3]
                             description = parts[4]
                             ingredients = parts[5].split(',') if parts[5] else []
                             ingredients = [ing.strip() for ing in ingredients]
                             dietary = parts[6]
                             try:
                                 avg_rating = float(parts[7])
                             except ValueError:
                                 avg_rating = 0.0
                             menu.append({
                                 'dishid': dishid,
                                 'name': name,
                                 'category': category,
                                 'price': price,
                                 'description': description,
                                 'ingredients': ingredients,
                                 'dietary': dietary,
                                 'avg_rating': avg_rating
                             })
             return menu
         
         
         def load_reservations():
             res_path = os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt')
             reservations = []
             if os.path.exists(res_path):
                 with open(res_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 10:
                             try:
                                 reservation_id = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 guestname = parts[2]
                                 phone = parts[3]
                                 emailaddr = parts[4]
                                 partysize = int(parts[5])
                                 date = parts[6]
                                 time = parts[7]
                                 specialrequests = parts[8]
                                 status = parts[9]
                                 reservations.append({
                                     'reservation_id': reservation_id,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'guestname': guestname,
                                     'phone': phone,
                                     'emailaddr': emailaddr,
                                     'partysize': partysize,
                                     'date': date,
                                     'time': time,
                                     'specialrequests': specialrequests,
                                     'status': status
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return reservations
         
         
         def load_waitlist():
             waitlist_path = os.path.join('data', 'waitlist.txt')
             waitlist = []
             if os.path.exists(waitlist_path):
                 with open(waitlist_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             try:
                                 waitlistid = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 partysize = int(parts[2])
                                 jointime = parts[3]
                                 status = parts[4]
                                 waitlist.append({
                                     'waitlistid': waitlistid,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'partysize': partysize,
                                     'jointime': jointime,
                                     'status': status
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return waitlist
         
         
         def load_reviews():
             reviews_path = os.path.join('data', 'reviews.txt')
             reviews = []
             if os.path.exists(reviews_path):
                 with open(reviews_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 reviewid = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 dishid = int(parts[2])
                                 rating = parts[3]
                                 reviewtext = parts[4]
                                 reviewdate = parts[5]
                                 reviews.append({
                                     'reviewid': reviewid,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'dishid': dishid,
                                     'rating': rating,
                                     'reviewtext': reviewtext,
                                     'reviewdate': reviewdate
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return reviews
         
         
         # Root route
         @app.route('/')
         def root_direct():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboards'))
         
         
         # Dashboard page
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboards():
             # For this example assume logged in user is 'john_diner'
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             users = load_users()
             menu = load_menu()
             reservations = load_reservations()
         
             username = current_user
         
             # featured_dishs: selecting first 3 dishes as featured for simplicity
             featured_dishs = []
             for dish in menu[:3]:
                 featured_dishs.append({
                     'dish_id': dish['dishid'],
                     'name': dish['name'],
                     'price': dish['price']
                 })
         
             # upcoming_reservationss: reservations for this user with status Upcoming
             upcoming_reservationss = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == current_user and r['status'].lower() == 'upcoming':
                     try:
                         time_int = int(r['time'].replace(':', ''))
                     except Exception:
                         time_int = 0
                     upcoming_reservationss.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'date_time': r['date'],
                         'time': time_int,
                         'party_size': str(r['partysize']),
                         'status': 1 if r['status'].lower() == 'upcoming' else 0
                     })
         
             return render_template('dashboards.html', username=username, featured_dishs=featured_dishs, upcoming_reservationss=upcoming_reservationss)
         
         
         # Menu page
         @app.route('/menu')
         def menu():
             menu_data = load_menu()
             menus = []
             for d in menu_data:
                 menus.append({
                     'dishid': d['dishid'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'category': d['category'],
                     'price': d['price'],
                     'description': d['description']
                 })
             return render_template('menu.htm', menus=menus)
         
         
         # Dish detail
         @app.route('/dish/<int:dish_id>')
         def dish_detail(dish_id):
             menu_data = load_menu()
             dish = None
             for d in menu_data:
                 if d['dishid'] == dish_id:
                     dish = {
                         'dishid': d['dishid'],
                         'name': d['name'],
                         'price': float(d['price']) if d['price'] else 0.0,
                         'description': d['description'],
                         'category': d['category'],
                         'ingredients': d['ingredients'],
                         'dietary': d['dietary'],
                         'avg_rating': int(round(d['avg_rating']))
                     }
                     break
             if dish is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('menu'))
             return render_template('dish_detail.html', dish=dish)
         
         
         # Make Reservation
         @app.route('/make_reservation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def make_reservation():
             # Assume current user is 'john_diner' and we have user info
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             users = load_users()
             user_info = users.get(current_user, None)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 guest_name = request.form.get('guestname', '').strip()
                 party_size = request.form.get('partysize', '').strip()
                 reservation_date = request.form.get('reservationdate', '').strip()
         
                 # Validate inputs
                 try:
                     party_size_int = int(party_size)
                     if party_size_int < 1 or party_size_int > 10:
                         raise ValueError
                 except Exception:
                     party_size_int = None
         
                 # Validate date format YYYY/MM/DD
                 try:
                     datetime.strptime(reservation_date, '%Y/%m/%d')
                     valid_date = True
                 except Exception:
                     valid_date = False
         
                 if guest_name and party_size_int and valid_date and user_info:
                     # Add the new reservation to reservations.txt
                     reservations = load_reservations()
                     new_id = 1 if not reservations else max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
                     # Time static or default, since not collected on form
                     time = '19:00'
                     status = 'Upcoming'
                     # Compose line to save
                     new_line = f"{new_id}|{current_user}|{guest_name}|{user_info['phone']}|{user_info['email']}|{party_size_int}|{reservation_date.replace('/', '-') }|{time}| |{status}\n"
                     # Save back including old data
                     res_path = os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt')
                     with open(res_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(new_line)
         
                     return redirect(url_for('dashboards'))
                 else:
                     # Invalid data submitted
                     return render_template('make_reservation.html', error='Invalid input')
         
             # GET
             return render_template('make_reservation.html')
         
         
         # My Reservations
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservation():
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             reservations = load_reservations()
             my_res = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == current_user:
                     try:
                         time_str = r['time']
                     except Exception:
                         time_str = ''
                     my_res.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'date': r['date'],
                         'time': time_str,
                         'party_size': str(r['partysize']),
                         'status': 1 if r['status'].lower() == 'upcoming' else 0
                     })
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservatons=my_res)
         
         
         # Cancel Reservation
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>')
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             reservations = load_reservations()
             res_path = os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt')
             updated = False
         
             new_lines = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == current_user:
                     # Mark status as Cancelled
                     r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                     updated = True
                 new_line = f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['guestname']}|{r['phone']}|{r['emailaddr']}|{r['partysize']}|{r['date']}|{r['time']}|{r['specialrequests']}|{r['status']}"
                 new_lines.append(new_line)
         
             if updated:
                 with open(res_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     f.write('\n'.join(new_lines) + '\n')
         
             return redirect(url_for('my_reservation'))
         
         
         # Waitlist
         @app.route('/waitlist', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def wait_list():
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             waitlist = load_waitlist()
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 party_size = request.form.get('partysize', '').strip()
                 try:
                     party_size_int = int(party_size)
                     if party_size_int < 0 or party_size_int > 10:
                         raise ValueError
                 except Exception:
                     party_size_int = None
         
                 if party_size_int is not None:
                     # Check if user already in waitlist active
                     found = False
                     for entry in waitlist:
                         if entry['username'] == current_user and entry['status'].lower() == 'active':
                             found = True
                             break
         
                     if not found:
                         new_id = 1 if not waitlist else max(w['waitlistid'] for w in waitlist) + 1
                         now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
                         new_entry = f"{new_id}|{current_user}|{party_size_int}|{now_str}|Active\n"
                         waitlist_path = os.path.join('data', 'waitlist.txt')
                         with open(waitlist_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                             f.write(new_entry)
                 return redirect(url_for('wait_list'))
         
             # GET
             # show position in waitlist for current user
             positions = [w for w in waitlist if w['status'].lower() == 'active']
             # Sort by jointime ascending
             positions.sort(key=lambda x: x['jointime'])
         
             position = None
             for idx, entry in enumerate(positions, 1):
                 if entry['username'] == current_user:
                     position = str(idx)
                     break
         
             return render_template('waitlist.html', position=position)
         
         
         # My Reviews
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_review():
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             reviews = load_reviews()
             menu = load_menu()
         
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['username'] == current_user:
                     dish_name = next((d['name'] for d in menu if d['dishid'] == r['dishid']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['reviewid'],
                         'dish_nme': dish_name,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['reviewtext']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)
         
         
         # Write Review
         @app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review():
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             menu = load_menu()
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 dish_id_str = request.form.get('dishid', '').strip()
                 rating_str = request.form.get('rating', '').strip()
                 review_text = request.form.get('reviewtext', '').strip()
         
                 # Validate rating 1-6 (spec says 6-1 but we interpret 1-6 range, accept 1 to 6)
                 try:
                     rating_int = int(rating_str)
                     if rating_int < 1 or rating_int > 6:
                         raise ValueError
                 except Exception:
                     rating_int = None
         
                 try:
                     dish_id = int(dish_id_str)
                 except Exception:
                     dish_id = None
         
                 if dish_id is not None and rating_int is not None and review_text:
                     reviews = load_reviews()
                     new_id = 1 if not reviews else max(r['reviewid'] for r in reviews) + 1
                     today_str = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     new_line = f"{new_id}|{current_user}|{dish_id}|{rating_int}|{review_text}|{today_str}\n"
                     reviews_path = os.path.join('data', 'reviews.txt')
                     with open(reviews_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(new_line)
         
                     return redirect(url_for('my_review'))
                 else:
                     dishes_list = [{'dish_id': str(d['dishid']), 'name': d['name']} for d in menu]
                     return render_template('write_review.html', dishes=dishes_list, error='Invalid input')
         
             # GET
             dishes_list = [{'dish_id': str(d['dishid']), 'name': d['name']} for d in menu]
             return render_template('write_review.html', dishes=dishes_list)
         
         
         # Profile
         @app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def profile():
             current_user = 'john_diner'
             users = load_users()
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
                 if email:
                     # Update user email in users.txt
                     users_path = os.path.join('data', 'users.txt')
                     # Update in memory
                     if current_user in users:
                         users[current_user]['email'] = email
                     # Rewrite file
                     with open(users_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         for u in users.values():
                             f.write(f"{u['username']}|{u['email']}|{u['phone']}|{u['fullname']}\n")
         
             userprofile = users.get(current_user, {'username': current_user, 'email': ''})
             return render_template('profile.html', userprofile=userprofile)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Utility functions for loading data
         
         def load_users():
             users = {}
             path = os.path.join('data', 'users.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             username, email, phone, fullname = parts
                             users[username] = {
                                 'username': username,
                                 'email': email,
                                 'phone': phone,
                                 'fullname': fullname
                             }
             return users
         
         
         def load_menu():
             menu = []
             path = os.path.join('data', 'menu.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 8:
                             try:
                                 dishid = int(parts[0])
                                 name = parts[1]
                                 category = parts[2]
                                 price = parts[3]
                                 description = parts[4]
                                 ingredients = [i.strip() for i in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5] else []
                                 dietary = parts[6]
                                 avg_rating = float(parts[7])
                                 menu.append({
                                     'dishid': dishid,
                                     'name': name,
                                     'category': category,
                                     'price': price,
                                     'description': description,
                                     'ingredients': ingredients,
                                     'dietary': dietary,
                                     'avg_rating': avg_rating
                                 })
                             except:
                                 continue
             return menu
         
         
         def load_reservations():
             reservations = []
             path = os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 10:
                             try:
                                 reservation_id = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 guestname = parts[2]
                                 phone = parts[3]
                                 email = parts[4]
                                 partysize = int(parts[5])
                                 date = parts[6]
                                 time = parts[7]
                                 specialrequests = parts[8]
                                 status = parts[9]
                                 reservations.append({
                                     'reservation_id': reservation_id,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'guestname': guestname,
                                     'phone': phone,
                                     'email': email,
                                     'partysize': partysize,
                                     'date': date,
                                     'time': time,
                                     'specialrequests': specialrequests,
                                     'status': status
                                 })
                             except:
                                 continue
             return reservations
         
         
         def load_waitlist():
             waitlist = []
             path = os.path.join('data', 'waitlist.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             try:
                                 waitlistid = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 partysize = int(parts[2])
                                 jointime = parts[3]
                                 status = parts[4]
                                 waitlist.append({
                                     'waitlistid': waitlistid,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'partysize': partysize,
                                     'jointime': jointime,
                                     'status': status
                                 })
                             except:
                                 continue
             return waitlist
         
         
         def load_reviews():
             reviews = []
             path = os.path.join('data', 'reviews.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 reviewid = int(parts[0])
                                 username = parts[1]
                                 dishid = int(parts[2])
                                 rating = parts[3]
                                 reviewtext = parts[4]
                                 reviewdate = parts[5]
                                 reviews.append({
                                     'reviewid': reviewid,
                                     'username': username,
                                     'dishid': dishid,
                                     'rating': rating,
                                     'reviewtext': reviewtext,
                                     'reviewdate': reviewdate
                                 })
                             except:
                                 continue
             return reviews
         
         
         
         # For demo, fixed current logged in username
         CURRENT_USER = 'john_diner'
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_direct():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboards'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboards():
             users = load_users()
             menu = load_menu()
             reservations = load_reservations()
         
             username = CURRENT_USER
         
             # featured_dishs (top 3 dishes)
             featured_dishs = []
             for d in menu[:3]:
                 featured_dishs.append({
                     'dish_id': d['dishid'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'price': d['price']
                 })
         
             # upcoming_reservationss for current user with status Upcoming
             upcoming_reservationss = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER and r['status'].lower() == 'upcoming':
                     try:
                         time_int = int(r['time'].replace(':', ''))
                     except:
                         time_int = 0
                     upcoming_reservationss.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'date_time': r['date'],
                         'time': time_int,
                         'party_size': str(r['partysize']),
                         'status': 1
                     })
         
             return render_template('dashboards.html', username=username, featured_dishs=featured_dishs, upcoming_reservationss=upcoming_reservationss)
         
         
         @app.route('/menu')
         def menu():
             menu_data = load_menu()
             menus = []
             for d in menu_data:
                 menus.append({
                     'dishid': d['dishid'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'category': d['category'],
                     'price': d['price'],
                     'description': d['description']
                 })
             return render_template('menu.htm', menus=menus)
         
         
         @app.route('/dish/<int:dish_id>')
         def dish_detail(dish_id):
             menu_data = load_menu()
             dish = None
             for d in menu_data:
                 if d['dishid'] == dish_id:
                     dish = {
                         'dishid': d['dishid'],
                         'name': d['name'],
                         'price': float(d['price']),
                         'description': d['description'],
                         'category': d['category'],
                         'ingredients': d['ingredients'],
                         'dietary': d['dietary'],
                         'avg_rating': int(round(d['avg_rating']))
                     }
                     break
             if dish is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('menu'))
             return render_template('dish_details.html', dish=dish)
         
         
         @app.route('/make_reservation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def make_resrvation():
             users = load_users()
             user = users.get(CURRENT_USER, None)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 guest_name = request.form.get('guestname', '').strip()
                 party_size = request.form.get('partysize', '').strip()
                 reservation_date = request.form.get('reservationdate', '').strip()
         
                 try:
                     party_size_int = int(party_size)
                     if party_size_int < 1 or party_size_int > 10:
                         party_size_int = None
                 except:
                     party_size_int = None
         
                 try:
                     datetime.strptime(reservation_date, '%Y/%m/%d')
                     valid_date = True
                 except:
                     valid_date = False
         
                 if guest_name and party_size_int and valid_date and user:
                     reservations = load_reservations()
                     new_id = 1 if not reservations else max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
                     time_str = '19:00'
                     status = 'Upcoming'
         
                     new_line = f"{new_id}|{CURRENT_USER}|{guest_name}|{user['phone']}|{user['email']}|{party_size_int}|{reservation_date.replace('/', '-') }|{time_str}| |{status}\n"
         
                     with open(os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(new_line)
         
                     return redirect(url_for('dashboards'))
                 else:
                     # Render make_reservation.html without context
                     return render_template('make_reservation.html')
         
             return render_template('make_reservation.html')
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def myreservation():
             reservations = load_reservations()
             myres = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER:
                     try:
                         time_int = int(r['time'].replace(':', ''))
                     except:
                         time_int = 0
                     myres.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'date': r['date'],
                         'time': time_int,
                         'party_size': str(r['partysize']),
                         'status': 1 if r['status'].lower() == 'upcoming' else 0
                     })
         
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservatons=myres)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>')
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservations = load_reservations()
             updated = False
             new_res = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USER:
                     r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                     updated = True
                 new_res.append(r)
         
             if updated:
                 # Save all reservations
                 with open(os.path.join('data', 'reservations.txt'), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in new_res:
                         line = f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['guestname']}|{r['phone']}|{r['email']}|{r['partysize']}|{r['date']}|{r['time']}|{r['specialrequests']}|{r['status']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
         
             return redirect(url_for('myreservation'))
         
         
         @app.route('/waitlist', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def wait_list():
             waitlist = load_waitlist()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 party_size = request.form.get('partysize', '').strip()
                 try:
                     partysize_int = int(party_size)
                     if partysize_int < 0 or partysize_int > 10:
                         partysize_int = None
                 except:
                     partysize_int = None
         
                 if partysize_int is not None:
                     # Check if user already in active waitlist
                     found_active = False
                     for w in waitlist:
                         if w['username'] == CURRENT_USER and w['status'].lower() == 'active':
                             found_active = True
                             break
         
                     if not found_active:
                         new_id = 1 if not waitlist else max(w['waitlistid'] for w in waitlist) + 1
                         now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
                         new_line = f"{new_id}|{CURRENT_USER}|{partysize_int}|{now_str}|Active\n"
                         with open(os.path.join('data', 'waitlist.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                             f.write(new_line)
                 return redirect(url_for('wait_list'))
         
             # GET: show position
             active_waits = [w for w in waitlist if w['status'].lower() == 'active']
             active_waits.sort(key=lambda x: x['jointime'])
             position = None
             for i, entry in enumerate(active_waits, 1):
                 if entry['username'] == CURRENT_USER:
                     position = str(i)
                     break
         
             return render_template('waitlist.html', position=position)
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_review():
             reviews = load_reviews()
             menu = load_menu()
             my_reviews = []
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['username'] == CURRENT_USER:
                     dishname = next((d['name'] for d in menu if d['dishid'] == r['dishid']), 'Unknown')
                     my_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['reviewid'],
                         'dish_nme': dishname,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['reviewtext']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=my_reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review():
             menu = load_menu()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 dish_id = request.form.get('dishid', '').strip()
                 rating = request.form.get('rating', '').strip()
                 review_text = request.form.get('reviewtext', '').strip()
         
                 try:
                     dish_id_int = int(dish_id)
                 except:
                     dish_id_int = None
         
                 try:
                     rating_int = int(rating)
                     if rating_int < 1 or rating_int > 6:
                         rating_int = None
                 except:
                     rating_int = None
         
                 if dish_id_int and rating_int and review_text:
                     reviews = load_reviews()
                     new_id = 1 if not reviews else max(r['reviewid'] for r in reviews) + 1
                     today_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     new_line = f"{new_id}|{CURRENT_USER}|{dish_id_int}|{rating_int}|{review_text}|{today_str}\n"
                     with open(os.path.join('data', 'reviews.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(new_line)
                     return redirect(url_for('my_review'))
                 else:
                     dishes = [{'dish_id': str(d['dishid']), 'name': d['name']} for d in menu]
                     return render_template('write_review.html', dishes=dishes)
         
             dishes = [{'dish_id': str(d['dishid']), 'name': d['name']} for d in menu]
             return render_template('write_review.html', dishes=dishes)
         
         
         @app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def profile():
             users = load_users()
             user = users.get(CURRENT_USER, {'username': CURRENT_USER, 'email': ''})
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
                 if email:
                     user['email'] = email
                     # Save back all users
                     with open(os.path.join('data', 'users.txt'), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         for u in users.values():
                             if u['username'] == CURRENT_USER:
                                 f.write(f"{u['username']}|{email}|{u['phone']}|{u['fullname']}\n")
